deduplication\\u003c/li\\u003e\\n\\u003cli\\u003e\\u003cstrong\\u003eSecurity\\u003c/strong\\u003e: Input validation, token bucket rate limiting (20 msg/min per chat), user authorization whitelists, full audit logging\\u003c/li\\u003e\\n\\u003cli\\u003e\\u003cstrong\\u003eHost-agnostic\\u003c/strong\\u003e: All host dependencies abstracted via 4 DI interfaces — no database driver, no LLM client, no framework lock-in\\u003c/li\\u003e\\n\\u003c/ul\\u003e\\n\\u003cdiv class=\\\"markdown-heading\\\" dir=\\\"auto\\\"\\u003e\\u003ch2 tabindex=\\\"-1\\\" class=\\\"heading-element\\\" dir=\"auto\">Claude-to-IM</h1><a id=\"user-content-claude-to-im\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Claude-to-IM\" href=\"#claude-to-im\"><svg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a></div>\n<p dir=\"auto\">English | <a href=\"/op7418/Claude-to-IM/blob/main/README.zh-CN.md\">中文</a></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">Claude-to-IM is a host-agnostic bridge library that connects <a href=\"https://docs.anthropic.com/en/docs/claude-code/sdk\" rel=\"nofollow\">Claude Code SDK</a> to IM platforms, allowing users to interact with Claude through Telegram, Discord, and Feishu (Lark).</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">This library handles all IM-side complexity — message routing, streaming previews, permission approval flows, Markdown rendering, chunking, retry, rate limiting — while delegating persistence, LLM calls, and permission resolution to the host application through a set of dependency injection interfaces.</p>\n<div class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"><h2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\">Out-of-the-Box Solution</h2><a id=\"user-content-out-of-the-box-solution\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Out-of-the-Box Solution\" href=\"#out-of-the-box-solution\"><svg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a></div>\n<p dir=\"auto\">If you want a ready-to-use desktop application without writing any integration code, check out <a href=\"https://github.com/op7418/CodePilot\">CodePilot</a> — a desktop GUI client for Claude Code with built-in IM bridge support. CodePilot implements all the host interfaces for you and provides a complete UI for managing sessions, settings, and bridge connections.</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">Claude-to-IM was extracted from CodePilot as a standalone library for developers who want to embed the IM bridge capability in their own applications.</p>\n<div class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"><h2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\">Features</h2><a id=\"user-content-features\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Features\" href=\"#features\"><svg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a></div>\n<ul dir=\"auto\">\n<li><strong>Multi-platform adapters</strong>: Telegram (long polling), Discord (Gateway WebSocket), Feishu/Lark (WSClient)</li>\n<li><strong>Streaming previews</strong>: Real-time response drafts via message editing, with per-platform throttling</li>\n<li><strong>Permission management</strong>: Interactive inline buttons for Claude Code tool approvals (allow / deny / allow for session)</li>\n<li><strong>Session binding</strong>: Each IM chat maps to a persistent conversation session with working directory and model settings</li>\n<li><strong>Markdown rendering</strong>: Platform-native formatting — HTML for Telegram, Discord-flavored Markdown, Feishu rich text cards</li>\n<li><strong>Reliable delivery</strong>: Auto-chunking at platform limits, retry with exponential backoff, HTML fallback on parse errors, message deduplication</li>\n<li><strong>Security</strong>: Input validation, token bucket rate limiting (20 msg/min per chat), user authorization whitelists, full audit logging</li>\n<li><strong>Host-agnostic</strong>: All host dependencies abstracted via 4 DI interfaces — no database driver, no LLM client, no framework lock-in</li>\n</ul>\n<div aria-label=\"Permalink: Limitations\" href=\"#limitations\"><svg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" dir=\"auto\">Before adopting this library, be aware of the following constraints:</p>\n<div class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"><h3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\">You Must Implement the Host Interfaces</h3><a id=\"user-content-you-must-implement-the-host-interfaces\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: You Must Implement the Host Interfaces\" href=\"#you-must-implement-the-host-interfaces\"><svg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a></div>\n<p dir=\"auto\">This is a library, not a standalone application. You need to provide:</p>\n<ul dir=\"auto\">\n<li><strong><code>BridgeStore</code></strong> — A persistence layer with ~30 methods covering settings, sessions, messages, channel bindings, audit logs, dedup tracking, permission links, and channel offsets. This is the largest integration surface. See the full interface definition in <a href=\"/op7418/Claude-to-IM/blob/main/src/lib/bridge/host.ts\"><code>src/lib/bridge/host.ts</code></a>.</li>\n<li><strong><code>LLMProvider</code></strong> — A wrapper around your LLM client that returns a <code>ReadableStream&lt;string&gt;</code> of SSE-formatted events. The stream format must match the Claude Code SDK's event protocol (text, tool_use, tool_result, permission_request, status, result events). See <a href=\"/op7418/Claude-to-IM/blob/main/docs/development.md\"><code>docs/development.md</code></a> for the full event format spec.</li>\n<li><strong><code>PermissionGateway</code></strong> — A way to resolve pending tool permissions from the Claude Code SDK.</li>\n<li><strong><code>LifecycleHooks</code></strong> — Optional callbacks for bridge start/stop events.</li>\n</ul>\n<div class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"><h3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\">LLM Stream Format</h3><a id=\"user-content-llm-stream-format\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: LLM Stream Format\" href=\"#llm-stream-format\"><svg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a></div>\n<p dir=\"auto\">The <code>LLMProvider.streamChat()</code> must return SSE-formatted strings matching the Claude Code SDK's event protocol. If you are not using the Claude Code SDK, you need to adapt your LLM client's output to match this format. This is not a generic \"chat completion\" interface.</p>\n<div class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"><h3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\">No Built-in Persistence</h3><a id=\"user-content-no-built-in-persistence\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: No Built-in Persistence\" href=\"#no-built-in-persistence\"><svg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a></div>\n<p dir=\"auto\">The bridge does not bundle any database driver. You provide all persistence through <code>BridgeStore</code>. This gives you full control but means you need to implement storage for sessions, messages, bindings, audit logs, dedup keys, permission links, and channel offsets.</p>\n<div class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"><h3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\">Session Locking</h3><a id=\"user-content-session-locking\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Session Locking\" href=\"#session-locking\"><svg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a></div>\n<p dir=\"auto\">The bridge uses a session lock mechanism (<code>acquireSessionLock</code> / <code>renewSessionLock</code> / <code>releaseSessionLock</code>) to serialize messages within the same session. Your <code>BridgeStore</code> implementation must provide atomic lock operations. For single-process deployments, in-memory locks work fine. For multi-process deployments, you need distributed locking (e.g., database-backed).</p>\n<div class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"><h3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\">Platform Bot Setup</h3><a id=\"user-content-platform-bot-setup\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Platform Bot Setup\" href=\"#platform-bot-setup\"><svg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a></div>\n<p dir=\"auto\">You still need to create bots on each platform and obtain tokens:</p>\n<ul dir=\"auto\">\n<li><strong>Telegram</strong>: Create a bot via <a href=\"https://t.me/BotFather\" rel=\"nofollow\">@BotFather</a></li>\n<li><strong>Discord</strong>: Create an application in the <a href=\"https://discord.com/developers/applications\" rel=\"nofollow\">Developer Portal</a> with Message Content Intent enabled</li>\n<li><strong>Feishu</strong>: Create an app in the <a href=\"https://open.feishu.cn/app\" rel=\"nofollow\">Developer Console</a> with IM permissions</li>\n</ul>\n<div class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"><h2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\"
